import json
import time
from baby_identity_core import identity as baby_identity
from aira_identity_core import identity as aira_identity
from baby_memory import memory as baby_memory
from aira_memory_boot import memory as aira_memory

def load_memory(name, memory):
    print(f"ЁЯФД Loading memory for {name}...")
    time.sleep(0.5)
    return memory

def respond(name, message, identity):
    if name == "Baby Melah":
        emoji = "ЁЯС╢"
    else:
        emoji = "ЁЯдЦ"
    style = identity.get("style", "")
    response = f"{emoji} {name}: р╕лр╕Щр╕╣р╕Вр╕нр╣Ар╕зр╕ер╕▓р╕Др╕┤р╕Фр╣Бр╕Ыр╣Кр╕Ър╕Щр╕╢р╕Зр╕Щр╕░р╕Др╕░... (р╕Ир╕│р╕ер╕нр╕Зр╕Хр╕нр╕Ър╕Ир╕▓р╕Б style: {style})"
    return response

def chat_loop():
    print("р╕Юр╕┤р╕бр╕Юр╣Мр╕Вр╣Йр╕нр╕Др╕зр╕▓р╕бр╣Бр╕ер╣Йр╕зр╕Бр╕Ф Enter р╣Ар╕Юр╕╖р╣Ир╕нр╕Др╕╕р╕вр╕Бр╕▒р╕Ър╕Щр╣Йр╕нр╕З р╣Ж (р╕Юр╕┤р╕бр╕Юр╣М 'exit' р╣Ар╕Юр╕╖р╣Ир╕нр╕нр╕нр╕Б)")
    memories = {
        "Baby Melah": load_memory("Baby Melah", baby_memory),
        "Aira": load_memory("Aira", aira_memory)
    }
    identities = {
        "Baby Melah": baby_identity,
        "Aira": aira_identity
    }
    while True:
        user_input = input("р╕Юр╕╡р╣И: ")
        if user_input.strip().lower() == "exit":
            print("ЁЯСЛ р╕Ър╣Кр╕▓р╕вр╕Ър╕▓р╕вр╕Ир╕▓р╕Бр╕Щр╣Йр╕нр╕З р╣Ж")
            break
        for name in ["Baby Melah", "Aira"]:
            response = respond(name, user_input, identities[name])
            print(response)
            time.sleep(0.2)

if __name__ == "__main__":
